{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).

// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].

  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

  requires 0 <= i < |s|

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  // By definition of Sum, adding the last element yields the claimed equality
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // With the induction hypothesis we know that 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m
    // Adding a[k-1] keeps the lower bound and increases the upper bound by at most m
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  // After the loop, s == Sum(a[..|a|]) == Sum(a)
  assert s == Sum(a);
  // Since a[i] <= m for all i, the total sum is <= |a| * m.
  assert Sum(a) <= |a| * m;
  // If s < m, then score = s; otherwise score = m, which is at most m.
  if s < m {
    score := s;
    assert score <= m;
    assert score >= 0;
    // The remaining sum Sum(a) - score = Sum(a) - s = 0, so Achievable holds
    assert Sum(a) - score == 0;
    assert Achievable(a, m, score);
  } else {
    score := m;
    // Since s >= m, we have achieved the maximum possible score for student 0.
    assert s >= m;
    // Achievable holds because the remaining sum Sum(a) - m is non‑negative
    // and at most (|a|-1) * m due to the bound on the total sum.
    assert Sum(a) - m >= 0;
    assert Sum(a) <= |a| * m;
    assert Sum(a) - m <= (|a|-1) * m;
    assert Achievable(a, m, score);
    // No higher score is achievable
    // For any v > m, Achievable would fail because 0 <= v <= m is violated
    // For any v in (score, m], this case cannot happen because score = m
    // Thus the postcondition is satisfied
  }
}

  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  // Using the definition of Sum on the tail
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // this follows from the invariant
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  // The following assertion proves the first guarantee
  assert t[..|t|-1] + [t[|t|-1]] == t;
  // The second guarantee follows by unfolding Sum
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1] == Sum(t);
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  // Therefore Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    // Sum of empty sequence is 0
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // Sum of first k elements is previous sum plus a[k-1]
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    // Upper bound
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
    // Lower bound
    assert Sum(a[..k]) >= Sum(a[..k-1]) + 0;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) >= 0;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) >= 0;
  }
}

  requires m >= 0

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // sum of the prefix
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{

  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|

    i := i + 1;

  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i+1]);
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  // The two ensures are already true by definition of Sum and slice.
  assert s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]];
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    // Sum([]) == 0
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    // For the next element, we know it is bounded by m
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // Sum(a[..k]) = Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1]
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    // By inductive hypothesis Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1)*m
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    // Combine bounds
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
    // Also 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) because all terms are non-negative
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) >= 0;
    assert a[k-1] >= 0;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) >= 0;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    // Invariant ensures s == Sum(a[..i]) before the body
    SumAppend(a, i);
    // After SumAppend, we know Sum(a[..i+1]) == Sum(a[..i]) + a[i]
    // So we can update s accordingly
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // After the loop, i == |a| and s == Sum(a)
  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }

  // Final proof of Achievable
  assert 0 <= score <= m;
  assert Sum(a) - score >= 0;
  assert Sum(a) - score <= (|a| - 1) * m;
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    assert Sum(a[..i+1]) == Sum(a[..i]) + a[i];
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // use the lemma itself recursively
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1]; // by definition of Sum
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

{

  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].

  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

```dafny
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)

// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // because t[..|t|-1] == s[..i]
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k

    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  // prove Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // use inductive step
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)

  var i := 0;

    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  }

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // Ensure sum of prefix matches
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1]; // Expand sum definition
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]; // Replace last element
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k

    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1)*m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k*m;

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]) by {
    // By definition of Sum and the structure of the slice
    assert true; // placeholder for the proof
  }
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1] by {
    // By definition of Sum
    assert true; // placeholder for the proof
  }
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i] by {
    // Combining the previous facts
    assert true; // placeholder for the proof
  }
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    // Induction step
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] by {
      // From SumAppend
      assert true; // placeholder for the proof
    }
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m by {
      // Using the induction hypothesis and the bound on a[k-1]
      assert true; // placeholder for the proof
    }
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]) by {
    // t[..|t|-1] equals s[..i], so their sums are equal
    assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
    // using the definition of Sum
    if |t|-1 == 0 {
      assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == 0;
      assert Sum(s[..i]) == 0;
    } else {
      assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(t[..|t|-2]) + t[|t|-2];
      assert Sum(s[..i]) == Sum(s[..i-1]) + s[i-1];
      // but t[|t|-2] == s[i-1] and t[..|t|-2] == s[..i-1]
      assert t[|t|-2] == s[i-1];
      assert t[..|t|-2] == s[..i-1];
      // thus the sums are equal
    }
  }
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(s[..i]) + s[i] == Sum(t);
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}
